    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_name VARCHAR(100),
    strategy_description TEXT
);


CREATE TABLE trade (
    trade_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    strategy_id INT,
    symbol VARCHAR(10),
    entry_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    exit_price DECIMAL(10,2),
    trade_date DATE,
    FOREIGN KEY (strategy_id) REFERENCES strategy(id)
);

    total_returns DECIMAL(10,2),

    total_trades INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (strategy_id) REFERENCES strategy(id)
